 Itthinaṃ viggahā vettha purisānañca viggahā  
  
      Migānaṃ viggahā vettha sakuṇānañca viggahā  
 Nāgarāje supaṇeṇa ca   maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Hatthānikaṃ rathānikaṃ asse patti dhajāni ca    
 Caturaṅginiṃ imaṃ senaṃ maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Hatthāruhe anikaṭṭhe rathike patatikārike  
 Balaggāni viyūḷhāni maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
                    
      Puraṃ uddāpasampannaṃ   bahupākāratoraṇaṃ  
 Siṅghāṭakesu bhumiyo maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Esikā parikhāyo ca palighaṃ aggalāni ca  
 Aṭṭālake ca dvāre ca maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Passa toraṇamaggesu nānādijagaṇā bahu  
 Haṃsā koñcā mayurā ca cakkavākā ca kukkubhā  
  
      Kuṇālakā bahū citrā sikhaṇḍī jivañjivakā    
 Nānādijagaṇākiṇṇaṃ maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Passa nagaraṃ supākāraṃ abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ  
 Samussitadhajaṃ rammaṃ suvaṇṇavālukasanthataṃ  
  
      Passa   tvaṃ paṇaṇasālāyo vibhattā bhāgasomitā  
 Nivesane nivese ca sandhibyubhe pathaddhiyo    
  
      Pānāgāre ca soṇḍe ca suṇā   odaniyāgharā  
 Vesī ca gaṇikāyo ca maṇimhi passa nimamitaṃ 
  
   Supaṇṇāva   machasaṃ   Vammine   machasaṃ syā   Uddhāpa   machasaṃ  aṭṭāla   syā 
   Jivajivakā   machasaṃ syā   Passettha   machasaṃ syā 
   Pathatthiyo   syā  pathaṭṭhiyo   machasaṃ   Saddā   syā  puvā   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Mālākāre ca rajake gandhike atha dussike  
 Suvaṇṇakāre maṇikāre maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Āḷāriye ca   sudace naṭanaṭṭakagāyake    
 Pāṇissare kumbhathunike maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
                    
      Passa bheri mutiṅgā ca saṅkhā paṇavadeṇḍimā    
 Sabbañca tālāvacaraṃ maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Sammatālañca viṇañca naccagītaṃ suvāditaṃ  
 Turiyatāḷitasaṃghuṭṭhaṃ maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Laṅghikā muṭṭhikā cettha māyākārā ca sobhiyā  
 Cetālike ca jalle ca maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Samajjā cettha vattanti ākiṇaṇā naranārihi  
 Mañcātimañce bhumiyo maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Passa malle samajjasmiṃ poṭhente diguṇaṃ bhujaṃ  
 Nihate nihatamāne ca maṇimhi passa nimmītaṃ  
  
      Passa pabbatapādesu nānāmigagaṇā bahu  
 Sihavyagghavarāhā ca acchakokataracchayo   
  
      Palasatā ca gavajā ca mahisā rohitā rurū  
 Phaṇeyyā ca varāhā ca gaṇino niṅkasukarā  
  
      Kadalimigā bahu citrā khiḷārā sasakaṇṇakā  
 Nānāmiggaṇākiṇaṇaṃ maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
                    
      Najjāyo supatitthāyo soṇṇavālukasanthatā  
 Acchā savanti ambuni macchagumbanisevitā  
  
      Kumbhilā makarā cettha suṃsumārā cakacchapā  
 Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā mañcarohitā 
  
   Āḷārike   machasaṃ syā   Gāyino   machasaṃ  gāyine   syā 
   Dindimā   machasaṃ   Taracchake   machasaṃ 
  
                    
  
      Nānādumagaṇākiṇṇā nānādijagaṇāyutā  
 Veḷuriyaphalakarodāyo   maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Passettha pokkharaṇiyo suvibhattā catuddisā  
 Nānādijagaṇākiṇṇā puthulomanisevitā    
  
      Samanodakasampannaṃ mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ  
 Upetaṃ vanarājehi   maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
      Purato videhe passa goyāniye ca pacchato  
 Kuruyo jambudipañca maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Passa candāñca suriyañca obhāsente   catuddisā  
 Sineruṃ anupariyanne maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Sineruṃ himavantañca sāgarañca mahiddhikaṃ    
 Cattāro ca mahārāja maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Ārāme vanagumbe ca pāṭiye ca   siluccaye  
 Ramme kimpurisākiṇṇe maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Phārusakaṃ cittalataṃ missakaṃ nandanaṃ vanaṃ  
 Vejayantañca pāsādaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Sudhammaṃ tāvatiṃsañca pāricchattañca pupphitaṃ  
 Pharāvaṇaṃ nāgarājaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Passettha devakaññāyo nabhā vijjurivuggatā  
 Nandane vicarantiyo maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Passettha devakaññāyo devaputtapalohinī devaputte caramāne maṇimhi passa 
 nimitaṃ  
  
                    
      Parosahassapāsāde veḷuriyaphalakatthate  
 Pajjalantaina vaṇṇena maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
   Veḷuriyakarodāyo   machasaṃ   Puthulomacchasevitā   machasaṃ 
   Rājihi   machasaṃ   Obhāsante   machasaṃ   Mahitalaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Piṭṭhiyeva   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Tāvatiṃse ca yāme ca tusite cāpi nimamite  
 Paranimamitābhiratino   maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
      Passettha pokkharaṇīyo vippasannodikā   suci  
 Mandālakehi saṃchantā padumuppalakehi ca  
  
      Dasettha rājiyo setā dasa   nīlā manoramā  
 Cha piṅgalā paṇṇarasā haḷiddā ca catuddasā  
  
      Visatiṃ tattha sovaṇṇā visatiṃ rajatāmayā  
 Indagopakavaṇṇābhā tāva dissanti tiṃsati  
  
      Dasettha kāḷiyo cha ca mañjeṭṭhā   paṇṇavisati  
 Missā bandhukapupphehi nīluppalavicittitā   
  
      Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ accimantaṃ pabhassaraṃ  
 Odhisuṅkaṃ mahārāja passa tvaṃ dipaduttama  
 Maṇikaṇḍo  
  
                    
      Upāgataṃ rāja upehi lakkhaṃ 
 Netādisaṃ maṇiratanaṃ tavatthi  
 Dhammena jiyyāma asāhasena 
 Jito ca no khippamavākarohi  
  
      Pañcāla paccuggata surasena 
 Macchā ca maddā   sahakekakehi  
 Passantu no te asaṭhena   yuddhaṃ 
 Na no sabhāyaṃ na kāroti kiñci  
  
                    
      Te pāvisuṃ akkhamadena mattā 
 Rājā kurūnaṃ puṇṇako cāpi yakkho  
 Rājā kaliṃ vicinaṃ aggahesi 
 Kaṭamaggahī puṇṇako nāma yakkho  
  
   Paranimmitavattino   machasaṃ syā   Vippasannodakā   machasaṃ syā 
   Dassanīyā   machasaṃ syā   Mañajaṭṭha   machasaṃ 
   Vicittataṃ   machasaṃ   Majjhā   machasaṃ   Assatthena   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Te tattha jute ubhatyā samāgate 
 Raññaṃ sakāse sakhinañca majjhe  
 Ajesi yakkho naraviriyaseṭṭhaṃ 
 Tatthappanādo tumulo babhūva  
  
                    
      Jayo mahārāja parājayo ca 
 Āyuhataṃ aññatarassa hoti  
 Janinda jinosi varaṃ dhanana 
 Jito ca me khippamavākarohi  
      Hatthi gavāssā maṇikuṇḍalā ca 
 Yaṃ cāpi mayhaṃ ratanaṃ pathavyā  
 Gaṇhāhi kaccāna varaṃ dhanānaṃ 
 Ādāya yenicchasi tena gaccha  
  
      Hatthi gavāssā maṇikuṇḍalā ca 
 Yañcāpi tuyhaṃ ratanaṃ pathavyā  
 Tesaṃ varo vidhuro nāma kattā 
 So me jito taṃ me avākarohi  
  
      Antā ca me so saraṇaṃ gati ca 
 Dīpo ca leṇo ca parāyano ca  
 Asantuleyyo mama so dhanena 
 Pāṇena me sadiso esa kattā  
  
                    
      Ciraṃ vivādo mama tuyhamassa   
 Kāmañca pucchāma tameva gantvā  
 Esova no vicaratu etamatthaṃ 
 Yaṃ vakkhati hotu kathā   ubhinnaṃ  
  
      Addhā hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi na ca māṇava sāhasaṃ  
 Tameva gantvā pucchāma tena tussāmubho janā  
  
      Saccannu devā vidahu kurūnaṃ 
 Dhamme ṭhitaṃ vidhuraṃ nāmamaccaṃ  
 Dāsosi rañño udavāsi ñātī 
 Vidhuroti saṅkhā katamāsi loke  
  
                    
      Āmāya dāsāmi bhavanti heke 
 Dhanena kītāpi bhavanti dāsā  
 Sayampi bheke upayanti dāsā 
 Bhayā paṇuntāpi bhavanti dāsā 
 Ete narānaṃ caturova dāsā  
  
   Tuyhañcassa   machasaṃ syā   Tathā   machasaṃ vi syā 
  
                    
      Addhā hi yonito ahampi jato bhavo ca rañño abhavo ca rañño  
 Dāsāhaṃ devassa parampi gantvā  
 Dhammena maṃ māṇava tuyhaṃ dajjā  
  
      Ayampi dutiyo vijayo mamajja 
 Puṭṭho hi kattā vivarittha pañhaṃ  
 Adhammarūpo vata rājaseṭṭho 
 Subhāsitaṃ nānujānāsi mayhaṃ  
  
                    
      Evaṃ ce no so vivarettha   pañhaṃ 
 Dāsohamasmi na ca khosmi ñāti  
 Gaṇhāhi kaccāna varaṃ dhaṇānaṃ 
 Ādāya yenicchasi tena gaccha  
 Akkhakaṇḍo  
  
      Vidhura vasamānassa gahaṭṭhassa sakaṃ gharaṃ  
 Khemā vutti kathaṃ assa kathannu assa saṅgaho  
      Avyāpajjhaṃ kathaṃ assa saccavādi ca māṇavo  
 Asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ kathaṃ pecca   na socati  
  
      Taṃ tattha gatimā dhitimā matimā atthadassimā  
 Saṅkhātā sabbadhammānaṃ vidhuro etadabravi  
  
      Na sādhāraṇadārassa na bhuñeja sādumekako  
 Na sece lokāyatikaṃ netaṃ paññāya vaddhanaṃ  
  
      Silavā vantasampanno appamatto vicakkhaṇo  
 Nivātavutti atthaddho surato sakhilo mudu  
  
                    
      Saṅgahetā ca mittānaṃ saṃvibhāgī vidhānavā  
 Tappeyya antapānena sadā samaṇabrāhmaṇe  
  
      Dhammakāmo sutādhāro bhatvayya paripucachano  
 Sakkaccaṃ paṭirupāseyya sīlavante bahussute  
  
      Gharamāvasamānassa gahaṭṭhassa sakaṃ gharaṃ  
 Khemā vutti siyā evaṃ evannu assa saṅgaho  
  
      Avyāpajjho   siyā evaṃ saccacavādi ca māṇavo  
 Asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ evaṃ pecca na socati  
 Gharāvāsapañho  
  
   Vicarittha   machaṣaṃ syā vi   Pacca   machasaṃ   Sādhu   machasaṃ syā vi 
   Abyāpajjaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Ehi dāni gamissāma dinno no issarena me  
 Mamevatthaṃ paṭipajja esa dhammo sanattano  
  
      Jānāmi māṇava tayāhamasmi 
 Dinnohamasmi tava issarena  
 Tihañca taṃ vāsayemu agāre 
 Yenaddhunā anusāsemu putte  
  
      Taṃ me tathā hotu vame tīhaṃ 
 Kurutaṃ bhavaṃ ajja gharesu kiccaṃ  
 Anusāsataṃ paputtadāre bhavajja 
 Yathā tayi pacchā   sukhī bhaveyya  
  
                    
      Sādhuti vatvāna pahutakāmo 
 Pakkāmi yakkho vidhurena saddhiṃ  
 Taṃ kuñajarājaññahayānuciṇṇaṃ 
 Pāvekkhi antopuramariyaseṭṭho  
  
      Koñcaṃ mayurañca piyañca ketaṃ 
 Upāgami tattha suramma rūpaṃ  
 Pahuta   bhakkhaṃ bahu antapānaṃ 
 Masakkasāraṃ viya vāsavassa  
  
      Tattha naccanti gāyanti avhayanti varā varaṃ  
 Accharā viya devesu nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
  
                    
      Samaṅgi katvā gāyanti avhayanti varā varaṃ  
 Antena pānena ca dhammapālo  
 Attatthamevānuvicintayanto 
 Pāvekkhi bhariyāya tadā sakāse  
  
      Taṃ candanagandharasānulittaṃ 
 Suvaṇṇajambonadanikkhasādisaṃ    
 Bhariyaṃ vacā ehi suṇohi bhoti 
 Puttāni āmantaya tambanette  
  
      Sutvāna vākyaṃ patino anujjā 
 Sunisaṃ vaca tambanakhī sunettaṃ  
 Āmantaya vammadharāni   cete 
 Puttāni indivarapupphasāme  
  
   Macca   machasaṃ   Bahutta   machasaṃ   Pamudāhi   machasaṃ syā 
   Sadisaṃ   machasaṃ   Dhammadharāni   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Te āgate muddhani dhammapālo 
 Cumbitvā putte acikampamāno  
 Āmantayitvāna avoca vākyaṃ 
 Dinnāhaṃ raññā idha māṇavassa  
  
      Tassajjahaṃ attasukhī vidheyyo 
 Ādāya yenicchati tena gacchati  
 Ahaṃ ca vo sāsituṃ āgatosmi 
 Kathaṃ ahaṃ aparittāya gacche  
  
      Sace vo rājā kurukhettavāsi   
 Janasandho puccheyya pahutakāmo    
 Kimābhijānātha pure purāṇaṃ 
 Kiṃ vo pitā anusāse puratthā  
  
      Samāsanā hotha mayāva sabbe 
 Konīdha rañño abbatiko manusso 
 Tamañajaliṃ kariya vadetha evaṃ 
 Māheva deva nahi esa dhammo  
 Viyaggharājassa nibhinajacco 
 Samāsano deva kathaṃ bhatvayya  
 Pekkhanakaṇḍo  
  
                    
      So ca mitte amacce ca ñātayo suhadaṃ jane  
 Alīnamanasaṅkappo vidhuro etadabravi  
  
      Ethayyo rājavasatiṃ nisīditvā suṇotha me  
 Yathā rājakulaṃ patetā yasaṃ poso nigacchati  
  
      Niha rājakulaṃ patetā aññāto labhatta yasaṃ  
 Nāsuro   napi   dummedho nappamatto kudācanaṃ  
  
      Yadāssa sīlaṃ paññañca soceyyañcādhigacchati  
 Atha vissasate tyamhi guyhañcassa na rakkhati  
  
      Tulā yathā paggahitā samadaṇḍā sudhāritā  
 Ajjhiṭṭho na vikampeyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
   Kururaṭṭhavāsi   machasaṃ syā   Bahuta   machasaṃ   Nātisuro   syā 
   Nāti   syā 
  
                    
      Tulā yathā paggahitā samadaṇḍā sudhāritā  
 Sabbani abhisambhonetā sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
                    
      Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ rājakiccesu paṇḍito  
 Ajjhiṭṭho na vikampeyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ rājakiccesu paṇḍito  
 Sabbāni abhisambhonto sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Yo cassa sukato maggo rañño suppaṭiyādito  
 Na tena vutto gaccheyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Na rañño samakaṃ   bhañeja kāmabhoge kudācanaṃ  
 Sabbattha pacchato gacche sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Na rañño sadisaṃ vatthaṃ na mālaṃ na vilepanaṃ  
 Ākappaṃ sarakuttiṃ vā na rañño sadisamācare  
 Aññaṃ kareyya ākappaṃ sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Kīḷe rājā amacechi bhariyāhi parivārito  
 Nāmacco rājabhariyāsu bhāvaṃ kubbetha paṇḍito  
  
      Anuddhato acapalo nipako saṃvutinduyo  
 Mano paṇidhisampanto sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
                    
      Nāssa bhariyāhi kīḷeyya na manteyya rabhogato  
 Nāssa kosā dhanaṃ gaṇhe sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Na niddantaṃ bahuṃ maññe   na madāya suraṃ pive  
 Nāssa dāye migaṃ   haññe sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Nāsasa pīṭhaṃ na pallaṅkaṃ na kocchaṃ na nāgaṃ   rathaṃ  
 Sammatombhīti ārūte sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
   Sadisaṃ   machasaṃ   Na niddaṃ bahumaññeyya   machasaṃ syā 
   Mige   machasaṃ syā   Nāvaṃ   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
      Nātidure bhave   rañño nāccāsante vicakkhaṇo  
 Samekkhaṃ cassa   tiṭṭheyya sandissanto sabhattuno  
  
      Na ve   rājā sakhā hoti na rājā hoti theno  
 Khippaṃ kujjhanti rājāno sukenakkhiva ghaṭṭitaṃ  
  
      Na pujito maññamano medhāvi paṇḍatā naro  
 Pharusaṃ patimanteyya   rājānaṃparisaṃ gataṃ   
  
      Laddhadvāro labhedvāraṃ neva rājusu vissase  
 Aggiva yato tiṭṭheyya   sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Puttaṃ vā bhātaraṃ saṃ vā   sampaggaṇhāti khattiyo  
 Gāmehi nigamehi vā raṭṭhe janapadehi vā 
 Tuṇhī bhūto upekkheyya   na bhane chekapāpakaṃ    
  
                    
      Hatthārūhe anīkaṭṭhe rathike pattikārake  
 Tesaṃ kammāvadānena rājā vaḍḍheti vetanaṃ    
 Na tesaṃ antarā gacche sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Cāpovunu    daro dhīro vaṃso vāpi pakampiyo  
 Paṭilomaṃ na vatetayya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Cāpovunudaro assa macchovassa ajivhavā     
 Appāsī    nipako suro sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Na bāḷhaṃ itthiṃ gaccheyya sampassaṃ tejasaṅkhayaṃ  
 Kāsaṃ sāsasaṃ daraṃ balyaṃ khiṇamedho nigacchati  
  
      Nātivelaṃ pabhāseyya na tuṇhi sabbadā siyā  
 Avikiṇṇaṃ mitaṃ vācaṃ patte kāle udiraye  
  
      Akkodhano asaṃghaṭṭho sacco saṇho apesuno  
 Samphaṃ giraṃ na bhāseyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
   Bhaje   machasaṃ syā   Samukhañcassa   machasaṃ   Name   machasaṃ syā 
   Paṭimanteyya   machasaṃ syā   Parisaṃkitaṃ   machasaṃ   Agigiva saṃyate tiṭṭhe 
  machasaṃ syā   Saputtaṃ vā bhātaraṃ vā   machasaṃ   Udikkheyya   machasaṃ  
   Thekapāpakaṃ   machasaṃ    Vetatanaṃ   machasaṃ syā    Vanu   machasaṃ 
    Ajivhatā   machasaṃ syā    Appasi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Mātāpettibharo assa kulejeṭṭhāpacāyiko  
 Bhirionatappasampanno   sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
                    
      Vinito sippavā danto katatto niyato mudu  
 Appamatto suci dakkho sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Nivātavutti vaddhesu sappatisso sagāravo  
 Surato sukhasambhāso sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Ārakā   parivajjeyya sahituṃ pahitaṃ janaṃ  
 Bhattā raññevudikkheyya anaññassa ca rājino  
  
      Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi sīlavante bahussute  
 Sakkaccaṃ paṭirupāseyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi sīlavante bahussute  
 Sakkaccaṃ anuvāseyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi sīlavante bahussute  
 Tappeyya attapānena sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi sīlavante bahussute  
 Āsajja paññe sevatha ākaṅkhaṃ sevetha ākaṅkhaṃ vuddhimattano  
  
      Dinnapubbaṃ na hāpeyya dānaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇe  
 Na ca kiñci nivāreyya dānakakāle vaṇibbake  
  
      Paññavā khuddhisampanno vidānavidikovido  
 Kālaññu samayaññu ca sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
                    
      Uṭṭhātā kammadheyyesu   appamatto vicakkhaṇo  
 Susaṃvihitakammanto sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Khalaṃ sālaṃ pasuṃ khettaṃ gantā cassa abhikkhaṇaṃ 
 Mitaṃ dhaññaṃ nidhāpeyya mitañca pācaye ghare  
  
   Saṇho sakhila sambāso   machasaṃ   Ākārakā   machasaṃ  
   Kāmadheyyesu   vi  
  
                    
      Puttaṃ vā bhātaraṃ saṃ vā sīlesu asamāhitaṃ  
 Anaṅgavā hi te bālā yathā petā tatheva te  
 Colañca nesaṃ piṇḍañca āsīnānaṃ   ca dāpaye 
  
      Dāse kammakare pesse   sīlesu susamāhite  
 Dakkhe uṭṭhānasampanne ādhipaccasmiṃ   ṭhāpaye  
  
      Sīlavā ca alolo ca   anuratto cassa rājino  
 Āvī raho hito tassa sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Chandaññu rājino assa   cittaṭṭho cassa rājino  
 Asaṅkusakavattissa sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
                    
      Ucchādaye ca   nahāpaye dhove pāde adhosiraṃ  
 Āhatopi na kuppeyya sa rājavasatiṃ vase  
  
      Kumbhampi pañajaliṃ kuriyā   vāyasaṃ   vā padakkhiṇaṃ  
 Kimeva sabbakāmānaṃ dātāraṃ dhiramuttamaṃ  
  
      Yo deti sayanaṃ vatthaṃ yānaṃ āvasathaṃ gharaṃ  
 Pajjunnoriva bhūtāni bhogehi mabhivassati  
  
      Esayyo rājavasati vattamāno yathā naro  
 Ārādhayati rājānaṃ pujaṃ labhati bhattusu  
  
 Rājavasatikaṇḍaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ samanusāsitvā ñātisaṅghaṃ vicakkhaṇo  
 Parikiṇṇo suhadehi   rājānamupasaṅkami  
  
                    
      Vanditvā sirāsā pade katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ  
 Vidhuro avaca rājānaṃ paggahetvāna añjaliṃ  
  
      Ayaṃ maṃ māṇavo neti kattukāmo yathāmatiṃ  
 Ñātinatthaṃ pavakkhāmi taṃ suṇohi arandama  
  
   Āsanānaṃ   machasaṃ   Pose   machasaṃ   Ādhipaccambhihi   machasaṃ 
   Alobhova   machasaṃ   Cassa   machasaṃ   Acchādaneva   machasaṃ 
   Kariyā   machasaṃ kayirā   syā   Cātaṃ cāpi   syā cāṭaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Subhajjehi   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Putte ca me udikkhesi yañca maññaṃ ghare dhanaṃ  
 Yathā pecca   na bhāyetha ñātisaṅgho mayi gate  
  
      Yatheva khalati bhumyā bhumiyāva patiṭṭhati  
 Evetaṃ khalitaṃ mayhaṃ etaṃ   passāmi accayaṃ  
  
      Sakkā na gantuṃ iti mayha hoti   
 Jhatvā vadhitvā idha kātiyānaṃ  
 Idheva hohi iti mayhaṃ ruccati 
 Mā tvaṃ agā uttamabhuripañña  
  
      Māheva dhammesu manaṃ paṇidahi 
 Atthe ca dhamme ca yutto bhavassu  
 Dhiratthu kammaṃ akusalaṃ anariyaṃ 
 Yaṃ katvā pacachā nirayaṃ vajeyya  
  
                    
      Nevesa dhammo na punetaṃ kiccaṃ 
 Ayiro hi dasassa raninda issaro  
 Ghātetuṃ jhāpetuṃ   athopi bhattuṃ 
 Na ca mayhaṃ kodhatthi vajāmi cāhaṃ  
  
      Jeṭṭhaputtaṃ upaguyha vineyya hadaye daraṃ  
 Assupuṇṇehi nettehi pāvisi so mahāgharaṃ  
  
      Sālāva sampamathitā   māḷutena pamadditā  
 Senti puttā ca dārā ca vidhurassa nivesane  
  
                    
      Itthisahasasaṃ bhariyānaṃ dāsisattasatāni ca  
 Khāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ vidhurassa nivesane  
  
      Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ vidhurassa nivesane  
  
      Hattharūhā   anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ vidhurassa nivesane  
  
      Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ vidhurassa nivesane  
  
  
   Pacchā   machasaṃ syā   Evaṃ   machasaṃ   Nasakakā gantuṃ mati mayhaṃ hoti   
 machasaṃ   Jāpetuṃ   machasaṃ   Jammapatitā   machasaṃ sampamadditā   syā   
 Hatthārohā   machasaṃ vi syā 
  
                    
      Itthi sahasasaṃ bhariyānaṃ dāsisattasatāni ca  
 Khāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā no vijahessasi  
  
      Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā no vijahessasi  
  
      Hattharūhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā vijahessasi  
  
      Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā no vijahessasi  
  
      Katvā gharesu kiccāni anusāsitvā sakaṃ janaṃ  
 Mittāmacce ca bhacce puttadāre ca bandhave  
  
      Kammannaṃ saṃvidhetvāna ācikkhitvā ghare dhanaṃ  
 Nidhiñca iṇadānañca puṇṇaṃ etadabravi  
  
      Avasī tuvaṃ mayha tīhaṃ agāre 
 Katāni kiccāni gharesu mayhaṃ  
 Anusāsitā putatadārā mayā ca 
 Karoma kaccāna yathā matiṃ te  
  
                    
      Sace hi katte anusāsitā te 
 Puttā ca dārā ca anujivino ca  
 Handehi dāni taramānarūpo 
 Dīgho hi addhāpi ayaṃ puratthā  
  
      Asambhitova gaṇhāhi ājāniyassa   vāladhiṃ  
 Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ tuyhaṃ jivalokassa dassanaṃ  
  
      Sohaṃ kissa nu bhāyissaṃ yassa me natthi dukkataṃ  
 Kāyena vācā manasā yena gaccheyya duggatiṃ  
  
      So assarājā vidhuraṃ vahanto 
 Pakkāmi vehāsayamantalikkhe  
 Sākhāsu selesu assajjamano 
 Kāḷāgiriṃ khippamupāgamāsi  
  
   Ājāneyyasasa   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Itthi sahasasaṃ bhariyānaṃ dāsisattasatāni ca  
 Khāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ yakkho brāhmaṇavaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati  
 Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ brāhmaṇavaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati  
  
 Hattharūhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ brāhmaṇaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati  
  
      Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ yakkho brāhmaṇavaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati  
  
      Itthi sahasasaṃ bhariyānaṃ dāsisattasatāni ca  
 Vejayantañca pāsādaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
 Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ brāhmaṇavaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati  
  
 Hattharūhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ brāhmaṇaṇṇe vidhuraṃ ādāya gacchati  
  
      Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatā  
 Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ paṇḍito so kuhiṃ gato  
  
                    
      Sace so sattarattena paṇḍito nāgamisasti  
 Sabbe aggiṃ pavekkhāma natthattho jivitena no  
  
      Paṇḍito ca viyatto ca vibhāvi ca vicakkhaṇo  
 Khippaṃ mocessatattānaṃ   mā hātha āgamissati  
 Antarapoyyālo  
      So tattha gantvāna vicintayanto 
 Ucacāvacā cetanakā   bhavanti  
 Imassa jivena nahatthi   kiñci 
 Hanatvānimaṃ hadayaṃ ādiyissaṃ  
    PAGE      
      So tattha lananvā pabbatamantarasmiṃ 
 Anto pavisitvā paduṭṭhacitto  
 Asaṃvutasmiṃ jagatippadese 
 Adhosiraṃ dhārayi kātiyāno  
  
      So lambamāno narake papāte 
 Mahabbhaye lomahaṃse vidugge  
 Asantasaṃ   kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭho 
 Iccabravī puṇṇakaṃ nāma yakkhaṃ  
  
   Khippaṃ mociya attānaṃ   machasaṃ   Cetanatā   machasaṃ 
   Mamatthi   machasaṃ syā   Assanatasanto   machasaṃ syā vi  
  
                    
  
      Ariyācakāsosi anariyarūpo 
 Asaññato saññatasantikāso  
 Accābhitaṃ kammaṃ karosi ludraṃ 
 Bhāve ca te kusalaṃ natthi kiñci  
  
      Yaṃ maṃ papātasmiṃ papātumicchasi 
 Konu tavattho maraṇena mayhaṃ  
 Amānusasseva te ajja   vaṇṇo 
 Ācikkha me tvaṃ katamāsi devatā  
  
                    
      Yadi te suto puṇṇako nāma yakkho 
 Rañño kuverassa hi so sajivo    
 Bhumindharo varuṇo nāma nāgo 
 Brahā sucī vaṇṇabaluppanno  
  
      Tassānujaṃ dhitaraṃ kāmayāmi 
 Irandatiṃ nāma sā nāgakaññā  
 Tassā sumajjhāya   piyāya hetu 
 Patārayiṃ tuyha vadhāya dhira  
  
      Māheva tvaṃ   yakkha ahosi muḷho 
 Naṭṭhā bahu duggahitena lokā  
 Kinne sumajjhāya   piyāya kiccaṃ maraṇena me iṅgha suṇoma sabbaṃ  
  
      Mahānubāvassa mahoragassa 
 Dhitukāmo ñātibhatohamasmi    
 Taṃ yācamānaṃ sasuro acoca 
 Yathā maṃ aññiṃsu sukāmanītaṃ  
  
                    
      Dajjemu kho te sutanuṃ sunettaṃ 
 Sucimbhitaṃ candanalittagattaṃ  
 Sace tuvaṃ hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa 
 Dhammena laddhā idhamāharesi 
 Etena vittena kumāri labbhā 
 Nāññaṃ dhanaṃ uttariṃ patthayāma  
      Evaṃ na muḷhosmi suṇohi katte 
 Na cāpi me duggahitthi kiñci 
 Hadayena te dhammaladdhena nāgā 
 Irandatiṃ nāgakaññaṃ dadanti  
  
   Tavajja   machasaṃ syā   Te   machasaṃ syā 
   Sajibbo   machasaṃ syā   Sumicchā   machasaṃ 
   Sumicchāya   machasaṃ   Haṭo   machasaṃ  
                    
      Tasmā ahaṃ tuyha vadhāya yutto 
 Evaṃ mamattho maraṇena tuyhaṃ 
 Idheva taṃ narake pātayitvā 
 Hanatvāna taṃ hadayaṃ ādiyissaṃ  
  
                    
      Khippaṃ mamaṃ uddhara kātiyāna 
 Hadayena me yadi te atthi 
 Ye kecime sādhunarassa dhammā 
 Sabbeva te pātukaromi ajja  
  
      Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭhaṃ 
 Nagamuddhani khippaṃ patiṭṭhapetvā  
 Asasatthamāsinaṃ samekkhiyāna 
 Paripucchi kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ  
  
      Samuddhaṭo mesi tuvaṃ papātā 
 Hadayena te ajja mamatthi kiccaṃ  
 Ye kecime sādhunarassa dhammā 
 Sabbeva me pātukarohi ajja  
  
      Samuddhaṭo tyasmi   ahaṃ papātā 
 Hadayena me nadi te atthi kiccaṃ  
 Ye kecime sādhunarassa dhammā 
 Sabbeva me pātukarohi ajja  
  
                    
      Yātānuyāyi ca bhavāhi māṇava 
 Addañca   pāṇiṃ parivajjayassu  
 Mā cassu mittesu kadāci dubhī 
 Mā ca vasaṃ asatīnaṃ nigacche  
  
      Kathannu yātaṃ anuyāyi hoti 
 Addañca pāṇiṃ dahate kathaṃ so  
 Asati ca kā ko pana mittadubbho 
 Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ  
  
      Asanthutaṃ   nopi ca diṭṭhipubbaṃ 
 Yo āsanenāpi nimantayeyya  
 Tasseva atthaṃ puriso kareyya 
 Yātānuyāyīti tamāhu paṇḍitā  
  
   Tusmi   machasaṃ   Allañca   machasaṃ syā    Assatthataṃ   syā asandhavaṃ   
 machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Yassekarattimpi ghare vaseyya 
 Yatthannapānaṃ puriso labhetha    
 Na tassa pāpaṃ manasāpi cetaye   
 Addañcapāṇiṃ   dahate mittadubbho  
  
      Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vā  
 Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbo hi pāpako  
  
      Puṇṇampi cetaṃ paṭhaviṃ dhanena 
 Dajjatthiyā puriso sammatāya  
 Laddā khaṇaṃ atimaññeyya tampi 
 Tāsaṃ vasaṃ asatinaṃ na gacche  
  
      Evaṃ kho yātaṃ anuyāyi hoti 
 Addañca   pāṇiṃ dahate punevaṃ  
 Asatī ca sā so pana mittadubbho 
 So dhammiyo hohi jahassu adhammaṃ  
 Sādhunaradhammakaṇḍaṃ  
  
                    
      Avasiṃ ahaṃ tuyha tīhaṃ agāre 
 Antena pānena upaṭṭhitosmi  
 Mitto mamāsi visajāmahaṃ ta   
 Kāmaṃ gharaṃ uttamapañña gaccha  
  
                    
      Api hāyatu nāgakulassa attho 
 Alampi me nāgakaññāya hotu  
 So tvaṃ sakeneva subhāsitena 
 Muttosi me ajja vadhāya pañña  
  
      Handa tuvaṃ yakkha mamampi nehi 
 Sasuraṃ nu te atthaṃ mayī carassu  
 Mayampi nāgādhipatiṃ vimānaṃ 
 Dakkhemu nāgassa adiṭṭhapubbaṃ  
  
      Yaṃ ve narassa ahitāya assa 
 Na taṃ pañño arahati dasasanāya 
 Atha kena vaṇṇena amittagāmaṃ 
 Tuvampicchasi uttamapañña anatuṃ  
  
   Labheyya   machasaṃ   Cittaye   machasaṃ syā 
   Alalañca   syā adubbhi pāṇaṃ   machasaṃ adubbhapāṇiṃ   sīmu aṭṭhakathā 
   Allañca   machasaṃ syā   Visajjāmaha taṃ   syā visajjemahantaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Addhā pajānāmi ahmapi etaṃ 
 Na taṃ pañño arahati dasasanāya  
 Pāpañca me natthi kataṃ kuhiñci 
 Tasmā na saṅke maraṇāgamāya  
  
                    
      Handa ca ṭhānaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ  
 Mayā sahā dakkhisi ehi katte  
 Yatthacchati naccagītehi nāgo 
 Rājā yathā vessavaṇo   naliññaṃ   
  
      Taṃ nāgakaññācaritaṃ gaṇena 
 Nikiḷitaṃ niccamaho ca rattiṃ  
 Pahutamālyaṃ   bahupupphachannaṃ   
 Obhāsati vijjurivantalikkhe  
  
      Antena pānena upetarūpaṃ 
 Nacceti gītehi ca vāditehi  
 Paripuraṃ kaññāhi alaṅkatāhi 
 Upasobhati vatthapiḷandhanena  
  
      So puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭhaṃ  
 Nisidayi pacchato āsanasmiṃ  
 Ādāya kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ 
 Upānayī bhavanaṃ   nāgarañño  
  
      Patvāna ṭhānaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ 
 Aṭṭhāsi kattā pacchato puṇṇakassa 
 Sāmaggipekkhī pana nāgarājā 
 Pubbeva jāmātaramajjhabhāsatha  
  
                    
      Yannu tuvaṃ agamā maccalokaṃ 
 Anvesamāno hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa 
 Kacci samiddhena idhānupatto 
 Ādāya kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ  
  
      Ayaṃ hi so āgato yaṃ tvamicchasi 
 Dhammena laddho mama dhammapālo  
 Taṃ passatha sammukhā   bhāsamānaṃ 
 Sukho bhave sappurisehi saṅgamo  
 Kāḷāgirikaṇḍaṃ  
  
   Vassavano   machasaṃ   Kaḷaññaṃ   machasaṃ   Bahuttamallaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Saccannaṃ   machasaṃ   Vasanaṃ   machasaṃ   Taṃ passa dhammaṃ samukhā   machasa 
  
                    
      Adiṭṭhapubbaṃ disvāna macco maccubhayaddito    
 Vyambhito nābhivādeti nayidaṃ paññavatāmiva  
  
                    
      Nacambhi vyambhito nāga naca maccubhayaddito  
 Na vajjho abhivadeyya vajjhaṃ vā nibhivādaye  
  
      Kathaṃ nu abhivāseyya abhivādāpayetha ve  
 Yaṃ naro hantumiccheyya taṃ kammaṃ na upapajjati  
  
      Evametaṃ yathā brūsi saccaṃ bhāsasi paṇḍita  
 Na vajjho abhivāseyya vajjhaṃ vā nābhivādaye  
      Kathaṃ nu abhivāseyya abhivādāpayetha ve  
 Yaṃ naro hantumiccheyya taṃ kammaṃ na upapajjati  
  
      Asassataṃ sassataṃ nu tavayidaṃ 
 Iddhījutī balaviriyupapatti  
 Pucchāmi taṃ nāgarājetamatthaṃ 
 Kathannu te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  
  
      Adhicca laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ te  
 Sayaṃ kataṃ udāhu dinnaṃ  
 Akkhāhi me nāgarājetamatthaṃ 
 Yatheva te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  
                    
      Nādhicca laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ me 
 Na sayaṃ kataṃ napi   devehi dinnaṃ  
 Sakehi kamemhi apāpakehi 
 Puññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  
  
      Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ 
 Kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko  
 Idadhijuti balaviriyupapatti 
 Idaṃ ca te nāga mahāvimānaṃ  
  
      Ahañca bhariyā ca manussaloke 
 Saddhā ubho dānapatī ahumahā  
 Opānabhūtaṃ me gharaṃ tadāsi 
 Santappitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca  
  
   Bhayaṭṭito   machasaṃ syā   No   sīmu   Nāpi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Mālañca gandhañca vilepanañca 
 Padīpiyā seyyamupassayañca  
 Acchādanaṃ sayanaṃ annapānaṃ 
 Sakkacca dānāni adamaha tattha  
  
      Taṃ me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ 
 Tassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko  
 Idadhijuti balaviriyupapatti idañca me dhira mahāvimonaṃ  
  
                    
      Evaṃ ce te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ 
 Jānāsi puññānaṃ phalupapatti  
 Tasmāhi dhammaṃ cara appamatto 
 Yathā vimānaṃ puna māvasesi  
  
      Nayidha santi samaṇabrāhmaṇā vā 
 Yesannapānāni dademu katte  
 Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ 
 Yathā vimānaṃ puna māvasema  
  
      Bhogī hi te santi idhupapantā 
 Puttā ca dārā anujivino ca  
 Tesu tuvaṃ vacasā kammanā ca 
 Asampaduṭṭho ca bhavāhi niccaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ tuvaṃ nāga asampadosaṃ 
 Anupālayaṃ vacasā kammanā ca  
 hatvā idha yāvatāyuṃ vimāne 
 Uddhaṃ ito gacchasi devalokaṃ  
  
                    
      Addhā hi so socati rājaseṭṭho 
 Tayā vinā yassa tuvaṃ sajivo  
 Dukkhupanitopi   tayā samecca 
 Vindeyya poso sukhamāturopi  
  
      Addhā sataṃ bhāsasi nāga dhammaṃ 
 Anuttaraṃ atthapadaṃ suciṇṇaṃ 
 Etādisiyāsu hi āpadāsu 
 Paññāyate mādisānaṃ viseso  
  
   Dukkhopaṇitopi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Akkhehi no tāyaṃ mudhā nu laddho 
 Akkhehi no tāyamajesi jute  
 Dhammena laddho iti tāya māha   
 Kathaṃ tuvaṃ hatthamimassamāgato  
  
                    
      Yomissaro tattha ahosi rājā 
 Tamayamakkhehi   ajesi jute  
 So maṃ jito rājā imassadāsi 
 Dhammena laddhosmi asāhasena  
  
      Mahorago attamano udaggo 
 Sutvāna dhirassa subhāsitāni  
 Hatthe gahetvāna anomapaññaṃ 
 Pāvekkhi bhariyāya tadā sakāse  
  
      Yena tvaṃ vimale paṇḍu yena bhattaṃ na ruccati  
 Na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo ayameso tamonudo  
  
      Yassa te hadayenattho āgatāyaṃ pabhaṅkaro  
 Tassa vākyaṃ nisāmehi dullabhaṃ dasasnaṃ puna  
  
      Disvāna te vimalā bhuripaññaṃ 
 Dasaṅguliṃ pañajaliṃ paggahetvā  
 Haṭṭhena bhāvena patītarūpā 
 Icchabravi kurūnaṃ kattaseṭṭhaṃ  
  
      Adiṭṭhapubbaṃ disvāna macco maccubhayaddito  
 Vyambhito nābhivādeti na idaṃ paññavatāmiva  
  
      Na vambhi vyambhito nāgi na ca maccubhayaddito    
 Na vajjho abhivādeyya vajjhaṃ vā nibhivādaye  
  
      Kathaṃ nu abhivādeyya abhivādāpayetha ve  
 Yaṃ naro bhantumiccheyya taṃ kammaṃ nupapajjati  
  
      Evametaṃ yathā brūsi saccaṃ bhāsasi paṇḍita  
 Na vajjho abhivādeyya vajjhaṃ vā nābhivādaye  
  
                    
      Kathaṃ no   abhivādeyya abhivādāpayetha ve  
 Yaṃ naro bhantumiccheyya taṃ kammaṃ nupapajjati  
  
   Māhu   machasaṃ   Tamāyamakkhehi   machasaṃ syā   Sayaṭṭito   machasaṃ syā   Nu 
   syā 
  
                    
      Asassataṃ sassataṃ nu tacayidaṃ 
 Iddhi juti bala viriyupapatti  
 Pucchāmi taṃ nāgakaññe tamatthaṃ 
 Kathannu te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  
  
      Adhicca laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ te 
 Sayaṃ kataṃ udāhu devehi dinnaṃ  
 Akkhāhi me nāgakaññe tamatthaṃ  
 Yatheva te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  
      Nādhicca laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ me 
 Na sayaṃ kataṃ napi devehi dinnaṃ  
 Sakehi kamemhi apāpakehi 
 Puññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ  
  
      Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ 
 Kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko  
 Idadhijuti bala viriyupapatti 
 Idaṃ ca te nāga mahāvimānaṃ  
  
      Ahañca kho sāmiko cāpi mayhaṃ  
 Saddhā ubho dānapatī ahumahā  
 Opānabhūtaṃ me gharaṃ tadāsi 
 Santappitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca  
  
      Mālañca gandhañca vilepanañca 
 Padīpiyā seyyamupassayañca  
 Acchādanaṃ sayanaṃ  mathannapānaṃ  
 Sakkacca dānāni adamaha tattha  
      Taṃ me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ 
 Tassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko  
 Idadhijuti balaviriyupapatti idañca me dhira mahāvimonaṃ  
  
                    
      Evañca te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ 
 Jānāsi puññānaṃ phalupapattiṃ  
 Tasmā hi dhammaṃ cara appamattā 
 Yathā vimānaṃ punamāvasesi  
  
   Sāyana   syā 
  
                    
      Nayidha santi samaṇabrāhmaṇā vā 
 Yesannapānāni dademu katte  
 Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ 
 Yathā vimānaṃ puna māvasema  
  
      Bhogī hi te santi idhupapantā 
 Puttā ca dārā anujivino ca  
 Tesu tuvaṃ vacasā kammanā ca 
 Asampaduṭṭho ca bhavāhi niccaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ tuvaṃ nāga asampadosaṃ 
 Anupālayaṃ vacasā kammanā ca  
 hatvā idha yāvatāyuṃ vimāne 
 Uddhaṃ ito gacchasi devalokaṃ  
  
      Addhā hi so socati rājaseṭṭho 
 Tayā vinā yassa tuvaṃ sajivo  
 Dukkhupanitopi tayā samecca 
 Vindeyya poso sukhamāturopi  
  
      Addhā sataṃ bhāsasi nāga dhammaṃ 
 Anuttaraṃ atthapadaṃ suciṇṇaṃ 
 Etādisiyāsu hi āpadāsu 
 Paññāyate mādisānaṃ viseso  
  
      Akkhehi no tāyaṃ mudhā nu laddho 
 Akkhehi no tāyamajesi jute  
 Dhammena laddho iti tāya māha 
 Kathaṃ tuvaṃ hatthamimassamāgato  
  
                    
      Yomissaro tattha ahosi rājā 
 Tamayamakkhehi   ajesi jute  
 So maṃ jito rājā imassadāsi 
 Dhammena laddhosmi asāhasena  
  
      Yadeva varuṇo nāgo pañahaṃ pucchattha paṇḍitaṃ  
 Tadeva nāgakaññāpi pañahaṃ pucchittha paṇḍitaṃ  
  
      Yatheva varuṇaṃ nāgaṃ dhīro tosesi pucchito  
 Tatheva nāgakaññampi dhīro tosesi pucchito  
  
                    
      Ubhopi te attamane viditvā 
 Mahoragaṃ nāgakaññañca dhīro  
 Acchambhi abhito alomahaṭṭho 
 Iccabravi varuṇaṃ nāgarājaṃ 
  
      Mā rodhayi nāga ayāhamasmi 
 Yena tava attho idaṃ sarīraṃ  
 Hadayena maṃsena karoti kiccaṃ 
 Sayaṃ karissāmi yathāmatinte  
  
      Paññā bhave hadayaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ 
 Tetyambha paññāya mayaṃ sutuṭṭhā  
 Anunanāmo labhatajja dāraṃ 
 Ajjeva taṃ kuruyo pāpayātu  
  
                    
      Sa puṇṇako annamano udaggo 
 Irandantiṃ nāgakaññaṃ labhitvā bhaṭṭhena bhāvena patītarūpo 
 Iccabravī kurunaṃ katta  seṭṭhaṃ  
  
      Bhariyāya maṃ tvaṃ samaṅgiṃ    
 Ahañca te vidhura karomi kiccaṃ  
 Imañca te maṇiratanaṃ dadāmi 
 Ajjeva taṃ kuruyo pāpayāmi  
  
      Ajeyyamesā tava hotu metti 
 Bhariyāya kaccāna piyāya saddhiṃ 
 Ānandi vitto sumano patīto  
 Datvā maṇiṃ mañca kayindapannaṃ  
  
      Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kantaṭṭheṃ 
 Nisidayī purato āsanasmiṃ  
 Ādaya   kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ   
 Upānayī   nagaraṃ indapantaṃ  
  
      Mano manussassa yathāpi gacche 
 Tatopi saṅkhippataraṃ ahosi  
 Sa puṇṇako kurunaṃ kataseṭṭhaṃ 
 Upānayī nagaraṃ indapantaṃ  
  
   Katatu   machasaṃ   Samaṅgi   machasaṃ   Ājaññamāruyha   machasaṃ 
   Vaṇṇaṃ   machasaṃ   Pakkamivehāsa   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Etindapannaṃ nagaraṃ padissati 
 Rammāni ca ambavanāni bhāgaso  
 Ahañca bhariyāya samaṅgibhuto 
 Tuvañca pantosi sakaṃ niketaṃ  
  
                    
      Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ katataseṭṭhaṃ   
 Oropiya dhammasabhāya majjhe  
 Ājaññamāruyha anomavaṇeṇā 
 Pakkāmi   vehāsayamantalikkhe  
      Taṃ disvā rājā paramappatito 
 Uṭṭhāya bāhāhi palissajitvā  
 Avikampayaṃ dhammasabhāya majjhe 
 Nisīdayi pamukhaṃ āsanasmiṃ  
  
      Tvaṃ no vinetāsi   rathaṃva naddhaṃ   
 Nandanti taṃ kuruyo dasasanne  
 Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ 
 Kathaṃ pamokkho ahu māṇavassa  
  
      Yaṃ māṇavotyābhivadī janinda 
 Na so manusso naraviriyaseṭṭha   
 Yadi te suto puṇṇako nāma yakkho 
 Rañño kuverassa hi so sajivo  
  
      Bhumindharo varuṇo nāma nāgo 
 Brahā suci vaṇṇabalupapanno  
 Tasasānujaṃ dhitaraṃ kāmayāno 
 Irandatī nāma sā nāgakaññā  
  
                    
      Tassā sumajjhāya piyāya hetu 
 Patārayittha maraṇāya mayhaṃ  
 So ceva bhariyāya samaṅgibhuto 
 Ahañcanuññāto maṇi ca laddho  
  
                    
      Rukkho hi mayhaṃ padvāre   sujāto 
 Paññākkhandho sīlamayassa sākhā    
 Atthe ca dhamme ca ṭhito nipāko 
 Gavapphalo   hatthigavasasachanto  
  
      Naccagitaturiyābhinādite 
 Ucchijjasenaṃ puriso abhāsi  
 So no ayaṃ āgato santiketaṃ 
 Rukkhassimassāpacitiṃ karotha  
  
   Ājaññamāruyha aṇomavaṇaṇaṃpakkami vehāsa mantalikekha   machasaṃ 
   Kattuseṭṭhaṃ   machasaṃ   Naraviraseṭṭha   machasaṃ syā 
   Pakkami   machasaṃ   Gharadavāre   syā pana dvāre   machasaṃ vi 
   Puna netāsi   machasaṃ   Sākho   machasaṃ 
   Rathaṃva raṭṭhaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Gavipaphalo   syā gavippalo   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Ye keci cittā mama paccayena 
 Sabbeva te pātukarontu ajja  
 Tibbāni katvāna upāyanāni 
 Rukkhassimasasāpacitiṃ karotha  
  
      Ye keci baddhā mama atthi raṭṭhe 
 Sabbeva te bandhanā mocayantu  
 Yathevayaṃ bandhanasmā pamutto 
 Imeva te muccare bandhanasmā  
  
                    
      Unnaṅgalā māsamimaṃ karontu 
 Maṃsodanaṃ brāhmaṇā bhakkhayantu  
 Amajjapā majjaraho   pipantu 
 Puṇṇahi thālāhi   palissutāhi  
  
      Mahāpathaṃ nicca samavabhayantu 
 Tibbañca rakkhaṃ vidahantu raṭṭhe  
 Yathaññamaññaṃ na vihaṭhayeyyuṃ 
 Rukkhassimassāpavitaṃ karotha  
  
      Orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 Bahuṃ antañca pānañca paṇḍitasasābhihārayuṃ  
  
      Hatthāruhā   anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā    
 Bahuṃ annañca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ  
  
                    
      Samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatā  
 Bahuṃ annañca pānañca paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ  
  
      Bahujjano   pasantosi disvā paṇḍitamāgate  
 Paṇḍitamhi anuppatte celukkhepo avatatthāti    
  
 Vidhurapaṇḍitajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  
   Rahā   machasaṃ syā   Pattikārikā   vi 
   Tālāhi   machasaṃ vi   Bahujano   machasaṃ 
   Hatthārohā   machasaṃ vi syā   Pavatatathāti   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
  
   Ummaggajātakaṃ 
                    
      Sabbasaṃhārako natthi suddhaṃ kaṅgu pavāyati  
 Alikaṃ bhāsatayaṃ dhutti saccamāhu mahallikā  
 Sattadārakapañhā  
  
                    
      Haṃsi tuvaṃ evaṃ maññesi seyyo 
 Puttena pitāti rājaseṭṭha  
 Handassatarassa te ayaṃ 
 Assatarassa hi gadrabho pitā  
 Gadrabhapañho  
 Ekunavīsatipañhā niṭṭhitā  
  
                    
      Nāyaṃ pure unnamati toraṇagge kakaṇṭako  
 Mahosadha vijānāhi kena thaddho kakaṇṭako  
  
      Aladdhapubbaṃ laddhāna addhamāsaṃ kakaṇṭako  
 Atimaññati rājānaṃ vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  
 Kakaṇṭaka pañho  
  
                    
      Itthi siyā rūpavati sā ca sīlavati siyā 
 Puriso taṃ na iccheyya sadadhāsi mahosadha  
  
                    
      Sadadhāmi mahārāja puriso dubbhago   siyā  
 Siri ca kālakaṇṇi ca na samonti   kudācanaṃ  
 Surikālakaṇṇi pañho  
  
                    
      Yesaṃ na kadāci bhūtapubbaṃ 
 Sakkhiṃ santapadampi imasmiṃ leke  
 Jātā amittā duve sahāyā 
 Paṭisandhāya caranti kissa hetu  
  
      Yadi me ajja pātarāsakāle 
 Pañhaṃ na sakkuṇeyyātha   vantumetaṃ  
 Raṭṭhā pabbājayissāmi   vo sabbe 
 Na hi mattho duppaññajātikehi  
  
   Dubhago   machasaṃ vi   Na samanti   machasaṃ   Sakkuṇetha   sīmu sakkuṇatha  syā 
   Pabbājayissāmi   sīmu  
  
                    
                    
      Mahājanasamāgamambhi ghore 
 Janakolahalasamāgamambhi jate  
 Vikkhittamanā anekacintā 
 Pañhaṃ na sakkuṇoma vattumetaṃ  
  
      Ekaggacittā ekamekā 
 Rahasigatā atthaṃ nicintayitvā    
 Paviveke sammasitvāna dhīrā 
 Atha vakkhanti janinda atthametaṃ  
  
                    
      Uggaputtarājaputtiyāna 
 Urabbhamaṃsaṃ piyaṃ manāpaṃ  
 Na te sunakhassa adenti maṃsaṃ 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  
  
      Cammaṃ vibhananti eḷakassa 
 Assapiṭṭhattharaṇasukhassa hetu  
 Na te sunakhassa attharatti 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  
  
                    
      Āvellitasiṅgiko hi meṇḍo 
 Na sunakhassa visāṇāni atthi  
 Tiṇabhakkho maṃsabhojano ca 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa  
  
      Tiṇamāsi pālasamāsi meṇḍo 
 Na sukho tiṇamāsi no palāsaṃ  
 Gaṇheyya suṇo sasaṃ khiḷāraṃ 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  
  
      Aḍḍhaṭṭhapādo   catuppadassa meṇḍo aṭṭhanakho adissamāno  
 Chādiyaṃ āharati ayaṃ imassa 
 Maṃsaṃ āharati ayaṃ amussa  
  
      Pāsādagato videhaseṭṭho 
 Vitihāraṃ aññamaññabhojanānaṃ  
 Addakkhi kira sakkhi taṃ janindo 
 Bhobhukkassa   ca puṇṇamukhasasa cetaṃ  
  
   Atthāni cittayitvā   machasaṃ syā   Aṭṭhaḍḍha   machasaṃ syā   Bobhukkassa   simu  
  
                    
                    
      Lābhā vata me anapparūpā 
 Yassa me edisā paṇḍitā kulambhi  
 Gambhiragataṃ   nipuṇamatthaṃ 
 Paṭivijjhanti subhāsitena dhīrā  
  
      Assatarirathañca ekamekaṃ 
 Phitaṃ gāmavarañca ekamekaṃ  
 Sabbaṃ vo dammi paṇḍitānaṃ 
 Paramappanitano subhāsitenāti  
  Dvādasanipāte   meṇḍakapañhaṃ  
  
                    
      Paññāyupetaṃ siriyā vihīnaṃ 
 Yasassinañcāpi apetapaññaṃ  
 Pucchāmi taṃ senaka etamatthaṃ 
 Kamettha seyyo kusalā vadanti  
  
      Dhīrā ca bālā ca bhatva janinda 
 Sippupapannā ca asippino ca  
 Sujātimantopi ajātimassa 
 Yassasino pessakarā bhavanti  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi 
 Pañño nihīno sirimāva seyye  
  
      Tavampi pucchāmi anomapañña mahosadha kevaladhammadassi  
 Bālaṃ yasassiṃ paṇḍitaṃ appahogaṃ 
 Kamettha seyyo kusalā vadanti  
  
                    
      Pāpāni kammāni karoti bālo 
 Idhameva seyyo iti maññamāno  
 Idhalokadassi paralokaṃ adassi 
 Ubhayattha bālo kalimaggahesi  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi 
 Paññova seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
      Na sippametaṃ vidadhāti bhogaṃ 
 Na bandhavā na sarīrāvakāso 
 Passeḷamugaṃ sukhamedhamānaṃ  
 Siri hi naṃ bhajate gorimanadaṃ 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi 
 Pañño nihino sirimāva seyyo  
  
   Pañhassa   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
                    
      Laddhā sukhaṃ majjati appapañño 
 Dukkhena phuṭṭhopi samohameti 
 Āgantunā sukhadukkhena phuṭṭho 
 Pavedhati vāricarova ghamme 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
      Dumaṃ yathā sāluphalaṃ   araññe 
 Samantato samabhicaranti pakkhi  
 Evampi aḍḍhaṃ sadhanaṃ sabhogaṃ 
 Bahujjano bhajati atthahetu  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva nihino sirimāva seyyo   
  
                    
      Na sādhu balavā bālo sāhasaṃ vindate dhanaṃ  
 Kandantameva   dummedhaṃ kaḍḍhanti niraye bhusaṃ  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
      Yā kāci najjo gaṅgamabhissavanti 
 Sabbāva tā nāmagottaṃ jahanti 
 Gaṅgā samuddaṃ paṭipajjamānā 
 Na khāyate iddhiparo   hi loko 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva nihīno sirimāva seyyo  
  
      Yametamakkhā udadhiṃ mahantaṃ 
 Samanti najjo sabbakālaṃ asaṅkhaṃ   
 So sāgaro niccamuḷāravego 
 Velaṃ na acceti hāsamudedā  
  
      Evampi bālassa pajappitāni 
 Paññaṃ na acceti siri kadāci 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
                    
      Asaññato cepi paresamatthaṃ 
 Bhaṇāti santhānagato   yasassi 
 Tasseva taṃ rūhati ñātimajjhe 
 Siri hi naṃ kārayate na paññā  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva nibhino sirimāva seyyo  
   Dhuva phalaṃ   machasaṃ   Kandantametaṃ   machasaṃ   Iddhi paññopi   machasaṃ 
   Masaṅkhyaṃ   machasaṃ   Saṇṭhānagato   syā 
  
                    
      Parassa vā antano vāpi hetu 
 Bālo musā bhāsati appapañño 
 So nindito hoti sabhāya majjhe 
 Peccāpi   so duggatigāmi hoti  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
                    
      Atthampi ce bhāsati bhuripañño 
 Anāḷhiyo   appadhano daḷiddo 
 Na tassa taṃ rūbhati ñātimajjhe 
 Siri ca paññāṇavato na hoti  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva nihino sirimāva seyyo  
  
      Parassa vā attano vāpi hetu 
 Na bhāsati alikaṃ bhuripañño 
 So pujito hoti sabhāya majjhe 
 Peccañca   so suggatigāmi hoti 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
      Hatthigavassā maṇikuṇḍalā ca 
 Nāriyo ca   iddhesu kulesu jātā 
 Sabbāva tā upabhogā bhavanti  
 Iddhassa posassa aniddhimanto 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
      Asaṃvihitakammantaṃ bālaṃ dummanta  mattinaṃ  
 Siri jahati dummedhaṃ jiṇṇaṃva urago tavaṃ  
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
                    
      Pañca paṇḍitā mayaṃ bhadante 
 Sabbe pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā 
 Tvaṃ no abhibhuyya issarosi   
 Sakko bhūtapatīva devarājā 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva nihīno sirimāva seyyo  
  
   Pacchāpi   machasaṃ syā   Anāliyo   machasaṃ syā 
   Pacchāpi   machasaṃ syā   Thiyo   machasaṃ 
   Dummedha   machasaṃ   Iriyasi   vi 
  
                    
      Dāsova paññassa yasassi bālo 
 Atthesu jātesu tathāvidhesu  
 Yaṃ paṇḍito nipuṇaṃ saṃcidheti 
 Sammohamāpajjati tattha balo 
 Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi  
 Paññeva seyyo na yasassī bālo  
  
                    
      Addhā hi paññāva sataṃ pasatthā 
 Kantā siri bhogaratā manussā  
 Ñāṇañca buddhānamatulyarūpaṃ 
 Paññaṃ na acceti siri kadāci  
  
      Yaṃ taṃ apucchimbha akittayi no 
 Mahosadha kevaladhammadassī 
 Gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ  
 Ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime 
 Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho 
 Dadāmi te gāmavarāni soḷaya  
  
 Visatinipāte sirimanda pañho  
  
                    
      Yena sattu bilaṅgā ca 
 Dviguṇapalāso ca pupphito  
 Yenādāmi tena vadāmi  
 Esa maggo yavamajjhakassa 
 Etaṃ chattapathaṃ vijānahi  
 Chattapathapañho 
  
      Hanti hatthehi pādehi mukhañca parisumbhati  
 Sace rāja piyo hoti kaṃ tenamabhipassati    
  
                    
      Ko nu santambhi pajjote aggipariyesanaṃ caraṃ  
 Addakkhi rattiṃ khajjotaṃ jātavedaṃ amaññatha  
  
      Svāssa gomayacuṇṇāni abhimatthaṃ tiṇāni ca  
 Viparitāya saññāya nāsakkhi sañajaletace    
  
      Evampi anupāyena atthaṃ na labhate mago    
 Visāṇato gavaṃ dohaṃ yattha khiraṃ na vindati  
  
   Kanetana tvābhipassati   machasaṃ   Pajjaletavenārada pajjeletave   machasaṃ sya 
   Mugo   syā 
  
                    
      Vividhehi upāyehi atthaṃ papponti māṇavā  
 Niggahena amittānaṃ mitatānaṃ paggahena ca  
  
      Seṇimokkhopalābhena   vallabhānaṃ nāyena ca  
 Jagatiṃ jagatipālā avasanti vasundharaṃ  
 Khajjopaṇaka pañho  
  
                    
      Sacca kira tvampi bhuripañño   
 Yā tādisi siri dhiti muti ca  
 Na tāyate bhāvavasupanītaṃ 
 Yo yāvakaṃ bhuñjasi   appasupaṃ  
  
      Sukhaṃ dukkhena paripācayanto 
 Kālakālaṃ   vicinaṃ chandachanto    
 Atthassa dvārāni avāpuranto 
 Tenāhaṃ tussāmi yavodanne  
  
      Kālañca ñatvā abhijihanāya 
 Mantehi atthaṃ paripācayitvā  
 Vijambhissaṃ   sihavijambhitāni 
 Tāyiddhiyā dakkhasi maṃ punāpi  
  
                    
      Sukhī hi eke   karonti pāpaṃ 
 Avaṇṇasaṃsaggabhayā puneke  
 Pahu samāno vipulatthivinti 
 Kiṃ kāraṇā me na karosi dukkhaṃ  
  
                    
      Na paṇḍitā antasukhassa hetu 
 Pāpāni kammāni samācaranti  
 Dukkhena puṭṭhā khalitattāpi   santā 
 Chandā ca dosā na jahanti dhammaṃ  
  
      Yena kenaci vaṇṇena mudunā dārunena vā  
 Uddhare dinamantānaṃ pacchā dhammaṃ samācare  
  
   Seni mokkhupalābhena   machasaṃ sonāmokkhapalābhena   syā 
   Atibhuripañña   machasaṃ   Bhuñji   machasaṃ   Kālānakālaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Channa   machasaṃ   Vijambhisaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Sukhipihete   machasaṃ syā   
 Khalitāpi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vā  
 Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbho hi pāpako  
  
      Yassā   hi dhammaṃ manujo vijaññā 
 Yecassa kaṅkhaṃ vinayanti santo  
 Taṃ hissa dipañca parāyaṇañca 
 Na tena mittaṃ jarayetha   pañño 
  
      Alaso gihī kāmabhogi na sādhu 
 Asaññato pabbajito na sādhu  
 Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī 
 Yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu  
  
                    
      Nisamma khattiyo kayirā nānisamma disampati  
 Nisammakārino rāja yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhati  
 Bhuripañho  
      Hanti hatthehi pādehi mukhañca parisumbhati  
 Sa ce rāja piyo hoti kaṃ tena mabhipassasi  
  
                    
      Akkosati yathākāmaṃ āgamañcassa na icchati  
 Sa ce rājā piyo hoti taṃ tena mabhipassasi  
  
      Abbhakkhāti abhutena alikena mabhisāraye sa ce rāja piyo hoti kaṃ tena 
 mabhipassasi  
  
  
                    
      Haraṃ antañca pānañca vatthasenāsanāni ca  
 Aññadatthu harā santā te ve rāja piyā honti kaṃ tenamabhipassasi  
 Devatāpucchita pañha  
  
                    
      Pañca paṇḍitā samāgatā 
 Pañehā me paṭibhāti taṃ suṇātha  
 Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā 
 Kassevāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ  
  
   Yassa hi   machasaṃ   Mitti jiyetha   machasaṃ mettiṃ   syā 
  
                    
      Tvaṃ no ācikarohi   bhumipāla 
 Bhattā bhārasaho tuvaṃ vadetaṃ  
 Tava chandañca ruciñca   sammasitvā 
 Atha vakkhanti   janinda pañca dhīrā  
  
                    
      Yā sīlavati anaññadheyyā   
 Bhattucchandavasānugā piyā manāpā  
 Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā 
 Bhariyāyāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ  
  
      Yo kicchagatasasa āturassa 
 Saraṇaṃ hoti gati parāyaṇañca  
 Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā 
 Sakhinovāvikaroyya guyhamatthaṃ  
  
      Jeṭṭho atha majjhimo kaṇiṭṭho 
 So ce silasamāhito ṭhitatto  
 Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā 
 Bhātuvāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ  
  
      Yo ve pitubhadayassa paddhagu   
 Anujāto pitaraṃ anomapañño  
 Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā 
 Puttassāvīkareyya guyhamatthaṃ  
  
      Mātā dipādā janindaseṭṭha 
 Yo taṃ poseti chandasā piyena  
 Nindiyamatthaṃ saṃsiyaṃ vā 
 Mātuyāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ  
  
                    
      Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhu 
 Na hi guyhassa pasatthamāvikammaṃ  
 Anipphādāya   saheyya dhīro 
 Nipphantattho yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya  
  
                    
      Kinnu tvaṃ vimano rājaseṭṭha 
 Dipadinda   vacanaṃ suṇoma netaṃ    
 Kiṃ cintayamāno dummanosi 
 Nuna deva aparādho atthi mayhaṃ  
  
   Tvaṃ ācikarohi   machasaṃ syā   Yā   machasaṃ syā 
   Rucini   machasaṃ syā   Anipphannatāya   machasaṃ syā 
   Vagganti   machasaṃ   Dvipada janinda   machasaṃ 
   Anaññatheyyā   machasaṃ syā   Metaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Pañño vajjho mahosadhoti 
 Āṇatto mevadhāya bhuripañño  
 Taṃ cintayanto   dummanosmi 
 Na hi devi aparādho atthi tuyhaṃ  
  
                    
      Abhidosagato idāni esi   
 Kiṃ sutvā kimāsaṃkate   mano te  
 Ko te kimavoca bhuripañña 
 Iṅgha taṃ vacanaṃ suṇoma brūhi metaṃ  
  
      Pañño vajjho mahosadhoti 
 Yadi te mantayitaṃ janinda dosaṃ  
 Bhariyāya rahogato asaṃsi 
 Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  
  
                    
      Yaṃ sālavanasmiṃ senako 
 Pāpakammaṃ akāsi asabbhirūpaṃ  
 Sakhinova rahogāto asaṃsi 
 Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  
  
      Pukkusapurisassa te janinda uppanno rogo arājayutto   bhātucca rahogato asaṃsi 
 Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  
  
      Ābādhoyaṃ   asabbhirūpo 
 Kāvindo naradevena phuṭṭho  
 Puttassa rabogato asaṃsi 
 Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  
  
                    
      Aṭṭhavaṅkaṃ maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 Sakko te adadā pitāmahassa  
 Devindassa gataṃ tadajja hatthaṃ 
 Mātucca rahogato asaṃsi 
 Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ  
  
      Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhu 
 Na hi guyhasasa pasatthamāvikammaṃ  
 Anipphādāya   saheyya dhīro 
 Nippannattho yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya  
  
   Vinatayamāno   machasaṃ syā vi   Ehisi   machasaṃ syā   Ki saṅkate   machasaṃ syā   
 Arājapatto   machasaṃ syā   Ābādhāyaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Anipphannatāya   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Na guyhamatthaṃ vivareyya rakkheyya naṃ yathā nidhiṃ  
 Na hi pātukato sādhu guyho attho pajānatā  
  
      Thiyā guyhaṃ na saṃseyya amittassa ca paṇḍito  
 Yo cāmisena saṃbhiro hadayattheno ca yo naro  
  
      Guyhamatthamasambuddhaṃ sambodhayati yo naro  
 Mantabhedabhayā tassa dasabhuto titikkhati  
  
      Yāvanto purisassatthaṃ guyhaṃ jānanti mantinaṃ  
 Tāvanto tassa ubbegā tasmā guyhaṃ na vissaje  
  
                    
      Vivicca bhāseyya divā rahassaṃ 
 Rattiṃ giraṃ nātivela pamuñce  
 Upassutikā hi suṇanti mantaṃ 
 Tasmā manto khippamupeti bhedaṃ  
  
 Visatinipāte pañcapaṇḍitapañehā  
                    
      Pañcālo sabbasenāya brahmadatto samāgato  
 Sāyaṃ pañcāliyā senā appameyyā sahosadha  
  
      Piṭṭhimatī pattimati sabbasaṅgāmekovidā  
 Ohārini saddavati bherisaṅkhappabodhanā  
  
      Lohavijjālaṅkārābhā   dhajini   vāmarohiṇi 
 Sippiyehi susampannā surehi suppatiṭṭhitā  
  
      Dasettha paṇḍitā āhu bhuripaññā rabhogamā    
 Mātā ekādasī rañño pañcāliyaṃ pasāsati  
  
                    
      Athetthekasataṃ khatyā anuyuttā yasassino  
 Acchinnaraṭṭhā byathitā pañcālīnaṃ vasaṃgatā  
  
   Alaṅkārā   machasaṃ syā   Vijini   machasaṃ   Rabhogatā   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Paṃvadā takkarā rañño akāmā piyabhāṇino  
 Pañcālamanuyāyanti akāmā vino gatā  
  
      Tāya senāya mithilā tisandhi parivāritā  
 Rājadhāni   videbhānaṃ samantā parikhaññati  
  
      Uddhaṃ tārakajātāva samantā parivāritā  
 Mahosadha vijānāhi kathaṃ mokkho bhavissati  
  
                    
      Pāde deva pasārehi bhuñja kāme ramassu ca  
 Hitvā pañcāliyaṃ senā brahmadatto palāyati   
  
                    
      Rājā panthavakāmo te ratanāni pavecchati  
 Āgacchantu tato dutā mañajukā piyabhāṇino  
  
      Bhāsantu mudukā   vācā yā vācā paṭinanditā  
 Pañcālā ca videhā ca uho ekā bhavantu te  
  
                    
      Kathannu kevaṭṭa mahosadhena 
 Samāgamo āsi tadiṅgha brūhi 
 Kacci te paṭinijjhanto kacci tuṭṭho mahosadho  
  
      Anariyarūpo puriso janinda  
 Asammodako thaddho asabbhirūpo 
 Yathā mugo ca badhiro ca na kiñcatthaṃ abhāsatha  
  
      Addhā idaṃ mantapadaṃ sududdasaṃ 
 Attho suddho naraviriyena   diṭṭho  
 Tathā hi kāyo mama sampavedhati   
 Hitvā sayaṃ ko parahatthamessati  
  
                    
      Channaṃ hi ekāva matī sameti 
 Ye paṇḍitā uttamabhuripattā  
 Yānaṃ ayānaṃ athavāpi ṭhānaṃ 
 Mahosadha tvampi matiṃ karohi  
  
                    
      Jānāsi kho rāja mahānubhāvo 
 Mahabbalo cuḷanibrahmadatto 
 Rājā ca taṃ icchati kāraṇatthaṃ 
 Migaṃ   yathā okacarena   luddo  
  
   Rājadhāniṃ   machasaṃ   Palāyiti   machasaṃ   Mudutā   machasaṃ 
   Naravirena   machasaṃ syā   Vedhate   machasaṃ   Magaṃ   machasaṃ  
   Okkacarena   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Yathāpi maccho khaḷisaṃ vaṅkaṃ maṃsena chāditaṃ  
 Āmagiddho na jānāti maccho maraṇamattano  
      Evameva tuvaṃ rāja cuḷaniyassa   dhitaraṃ  
 Kāmagiddho na jānasi macchova maraṇamatatano  
  
      Sace gacchasi pañcālaṃ khippamantaṃ jahissasi  
 Migaṃ pathānupannaṃva   mahannaṃ bhayamessati  
  
                    
  
      Mayameva bālambase eḷamugā 
 Ye uttamatthāni tayī lapimbha  
 Kimeva tvaṃ naṅgalakoṭivaddho   
 Atthāni jānāsi yathāpi aññe  
  
      Imaṃ gale gahetvāna nāsetha vijitā mama  
 Yo me ratanalābhassa antarāyāya bhāsati  
  
                    
      Tato ca so apakkamma vedehassa upantikā  
 Atha āmantayī dutaṃ māḍharaṃ   suvapaṇḍataṃ  
  
      Ehi samma haripakkha   veyyāvaccaṃ karohi me  
 Atthi pañcālarājassa sāḷikā sayanapālikā  
  
      Taṃ pattharena   pucchassu sā hi sabbassa kovidā  
 Sā tesaṃ sabbaṃ jānāti rañño ca kosiyassa ca  
  
      Āmoti so paṭissutvā māḍharo suvapaṇḍito  
 Agamāsi haripakkho sāḷikāya upantikaṃ  
  
      Tato ca kho so gantvāna māḍharo suvapaṇḍito  
 Atha āmantayi sugharaṃ sāḷikaṃ mañajubhāṇikaṃ  
  
      Kacci te sughare khamanīyaṃ kacci vesse   anāmayaṃ  
 Kacci te madhunā lājā labbhate sughare tava  
  
      Kusalañceva me samma atho samma anāmayaṃ  
 Atho me madhunā lājā labbhate suvapaṇḍite  
  
   Cuḷaneyyassa   machasaṃ   Panthānu   machasaṃ vi   Vaḍḍho   machasaṃ 
   Mādharaṃ   machasaṃ mādhuraṃ   syā   Haritapakkha   machasaṃ syā 
   Bandhanena   machasaṃ pattharane   syā satthacena   syā   Vese   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Kuto nu samma āgamma kassa vā pahito tuvaṃ  
 Na ca mesi ito pubbe diṭṭho vā yadi vā suto  
  
                    
      Ahosiṃ sivirājassa pāsādo sayanapālako  
 Tato so dhammiko rājā baddhe   mocesi bandhaṇā  
  
                    
      Tassa mekā dutiyāsi sāḷikā ñajubhāṇikā  
 Taṃ tattha avadhi seno pekkhato sughare mama  
      Tassā kāmā hi sammatto āgatosmi tavantike  
 Sace kareyyasi okāsaṃ ubhatyāva vasāmese  
  
                    
      Suvoca suviṃ kāmeyya sāḷiko pana sāḷikaṃ  
 Suvassa sāḷikāya ca   saṃvāso hoti kidiso  
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ kāmi kāmayati   api caṇḍālikāmapi  
 Sabbhi sadiso hoti natthi kāme asādiso  
  
      Atthi jambāvati nāma mātā sivissa   rājino  
 Sā bhariyā vāsudevassa kaṇhassa mahesī piyā  
  
                    
      Rathāvati kimpurisi sāpi vacchaṃ akāmayi  
 Manusso migiyā saddhiṃ natthi kāme asādiso  
  
      Handa khohaṃ gamisasāmi sāḷike maṃjubhāṇike  
 Paccakkhānupadaṃ hetaṃ atimaññasi nūna maṃ  
  
                    
      Na siri taramānassa māḍhara suvapaṇḍata  
 Idheva tāva acchassu yāva rājānaṃ dakkhasi  
 Sossasi   saddaṃ mutiṅgānaṃ ānubhāvañca rājino  
  
      Yo nu khoyaṃ tibbo saddo tirojanapade suto  
 Dhitā pañcālarājassa osadhi viya vaṇṇinī  
 Taṃ dassati videhānaṃ so vivāho bhavissati  
  
                    
      Nediso   te amittānaṃ vivāho hotu māḍhara  
 Yathā pañcālarājassa vedehena bhavissati  
  
   Banedha   machasaṃ   Sāḷikāyeva   machasaṃ   Yoyaṃ kāme kāmayati   machasaṃ syā 
   Sibbissa   aṭṭhakathā   Sosi   machasaṃ syā 
   Ediso   machasaṃ syā vi  
  
                    
      Ānayitvāna vedehaṃ pañcālānaṃ rathesabho  
 Tato naṃ ghātayisasti nāssa sakkhi bhavissati  
  
                    
      Handa kho maṃ anujānāhi rattiyo sattamattiyo  
 Yāvāhaṃ sivirājassa ārocemi mahosino  
 Laddho ca me āvasatho sāḷikāya upantikaṃ  
      Handa kho taṃ anujānāmi rattiyo sattamattiyo  
 Sace tvaṃ sattarattena nāgacchasi mamantike  
 Maññe okkantasattaṃ maṃ matāya āgamissasi  
  
      Tato ca kho so gantvāna māḍharo suvapaṇḍito  
 Mahosadhassa akkhāsi sāḷiyā   vacanaṃ idaṃ  
  
                    
      Yasseva ghare bhuñejayya bhogaṃ  
 Tasseva atthaṃ puriso careyya  
  
      Bhandāhaṃ gacchāmi pure janinda  
 Pañcālarājassa puraṃ surammaṃ  
 Nivesanāni māpetuṃ vedehasasa yasassino  
  
      Nivesanāni māpetvā vedehasasa yasassino  
 Yadā te pahiṇeyyāmi tadā eyyāsi khattiya  
  
                    
      Tato ca pāyāsi pure māhosadho  
 Pañcālarājassa puraṃ surammaṃ  
 Nivesanāni māpetuṃ vedehasasa yasassino  
  
                    
      Nivesanāni māpetvā vedehasasa yasassino  
 Athassa pahiṇi dutaṃ  vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  
 Ehidāni mahārāja māpitaṃ te nivesanaṃ  
  
      Tato ca rājā pāyāsi senāya caturaṅgiyā  
 Anantavāhanaṃ daṭṭhuṃ phītaṃ kampilliyaṃ puraṃ  
  
      Tato ca kho so gantvāna brahmadantassa pāhiṇi  
 Āgatosmi mahārāja tava pādāni vandituṃ  
  
      Dadāhidāni me bhariyaṃ nāriṃ sabbaṅgasobhiniṃ  
 Suvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ  
  
                    
      Svāgataṃ te vedeha atho te adurāgataṃ  
 Nakkhattaññeca paripuccha ahaṃ kaññaṃ dadāmi te  
 Suvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ  
  
   Sāḷikāya   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Tato ca rājā vedeho nakkhantaṃ paripucchatha  
 Nakkhantaṃ paripucchitvā brahmadantasasa pāhiṇi  
  
      Dadāhidāni me bhariyaṃ nāriṃ sabbaṅgasobhiniṃ  
 Suvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ  
  
      Dadāhidāni me bhariyaṃ nāriṃ sabbaṅgasobhiniṃ  
 Suvaṇṇena paṭicchannaṃ dāsīgaṇapukkhataṃ  
  
      Hatthi assā rathā patti senā tiṭṭhanti vammitā    
 Ukkā padintā jhāyanti kinnu maññanti paṇḍitā  
  
                    
      Hatthi assā rathā patti senā tiṭṭhanti vammitā  
 Ukkā padintā jhāyanti kinnu kāhanti paṇḍitā  
  
                    
      Rakkhati taṃ mahārāja cuḷaniyo mahabbalo  
 Paduṭṭho te brahmadatto pāto taṃ ghātayissati  
  
       Ubbedhate   me hadayaṃ mukhañca parisussati  
 Nibbutiṃ nādhigacchāmi aggidaḍḍhova ātape  
  
      Kammārānaṃ yathā ukkā anto jhāyati no bahi  
 Evampi hadayaṃ mayhaṃ anto jhāyati no bahi  
  
      Pamatto mantanātito bhintamantosi khantiya  
 Idāni kho taṃ tāyantu paṇḍitā mantino janā  
  
      Akatvāmaccassa vacanaṃ atthakāmahitesino  
 Antapitirato rāja migo kuṭeva ohito  
  
      Yathāpi maccho baḷisaṃ maṅkaṃ maṃsena chācitaṃ  
 Āmagiddho na jānāti maccho maraṇamattano  
  
      Evameva tuvaṃ rāja cuḷaneyyassa dhitaraṃ  
 Kāmagiddho na jānāsi macchova maraṇamattano  
  
      Sace gacchasi pañcālaṃ khippamattaṃ   jahessasi    
 Migaṃ pathānupantaṃva   mahantaṃ bhayamessati   
  
   Vammikā   machasaṃ   Ubbedhati   machasaṃ vi   Khippamatthaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Jahissasi   machasaṃ syā   Patthānu   machasaṃ syā   Bhayamesassi   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Anariyarūpo puriso janinda 
 Abhiva ucchaṅgagato isayye    
 Na tena mettiṃ kayirātha dhīro 
 Dukkho have kāpurisena   saṅgamo  
  
                    
      Yantveva   jaññā purisaṃ janinda 
 Silavāyaṃ bahusasuto  
 Teneva tettiṃ kayirātha dhīro 
 Sukho bhave sappurisena saṅgamo  
  
      Bālo tuvaṃ phaḷamugosi rāja 
 Yo uttamatthāni mayī lapittho  
 Kimevāhaṃ naṅgalakoṭivaddho 
 Atthāni jānissaṃ yathāpi aññe  
  
      Imaṃ gale gahetvana nāsetha vijitā mama  
 Yo me ratanalābhassa antarāyāya bhāsati  
  
                    
      Mahosadha atitena nānuvijjhanti paṇḍitā  
 Ki maṃ assaṃ ca sambaddhaṃ   patodeneva vijjhasi  
  
      Sace passasi mokkhaṃ me   khemaṃ vā pana pasasasi  
 Teneva maṃ anusāsa kiṃ atitena vijjhasi 
  
      Atitaṃ mānusaṃ kammaṃ dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃ  
 Na taṃ sakkomi mocetuṃ tvampi jānassu khattiya  
  
      Santi vehāsayā   nāgā iddhimanto yasassino  
 Tepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā  
  
      Santi vehāsayā assā iddhimanto yasassino  
 Tepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā  
  
      Santi vehāsayā pakkhī iddhimanto yasassino  
 Tepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā  
  
      Santi vehāsayā yakkhā iddhimanto yasassino  
 Tepi ādāya gaccheyyuṃ yassa honti tathāvidhā  
  
   Ḍaṃseyya   machasaṃ syā   Kāpurisehi   machasaṃ   Yadeva   machasaṃ 
   Puriso   machasaṃ   Sambandhaṃ   machasaṃ   Vā   machasaṃ 
   Vehāyasā   machasaṃ syā vehāsasā   vi 
  
                    
      Atitaṃ mānusaṃ   kammaṃ dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃ  
 Na taṃ sakkomi mocetuṃ antalikkhena khattiya  
  
                    
  
      Atiradassi puriso mahante udakaṇṇave  
 Yattha so labhate gādhaṃ   tattha so vindate sukhaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ ambhañca añño ca tvaṃ patiṭṭhā mahosadha  
 Tvaṃ nosi mantinaṃ seṭṭho ambhe dukkhā pamocaya  
  
      Atitaṃ mānusaṃ kammaṃ dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃ  
 Na taṃ sakkomi mocetuṃ tvampi rānassu   senaka  
  
      Suṇohi metaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃ  
 Senakaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi  
  
                    
      Aggiṃ dvārato dema gaṇhāmase vikatatanaṃ    
 Aññamaññaṃ vadhitvāna khippaṃ hessāma jīvitaṃ  
 Mā no rājā   brahmadatto ciraṃ dukkhena mārayi  
  
      Suṇohi etaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃ  
 Pukkusaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi  
  
      Visaṃ khāditvā miyyāma khippaṃ hessāma jīvitaṃ  
 Mā no rājā brahamadatto ciraṃ dukkhena mārayi

 Kāvindaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi

 Mā no rājā buhmadatto ciraṃ dukkhena mārayi  
  
      Suṇohi etaṃ vacanaṃ passasetaṃ mahabbhayaṃ  
 Devindaṃdāni pucchāmi kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi  
  
      Aggiṃ dvārato dema gaṇhāmase vikatatanaṃ    
 Aññamaññaṃ vadhitvāna khippaṃ hessāma jīvitaṃ  
 Na no sakkoti mocetuṃ sukheneva mahosadho  
  
                    
      Yathā kadalino sāraṃ anevasaṃ nādhigacchati  
 Evaṃ anevasamānā naṃ pañahaṃ nājjhagamāmase

   Vikantanaṃ   machasaṃ syā

 Evaṃ anvesamānāṃ pañhaṃ nājjhagamāmase

 Sakāse dummanussānaṃ bālānamavijānataṃ

 Evampi hadayaṃ mayhaṃ anto jhayati no bahi

 Vedehaṃ dukkhitaṃ disvā idaṃ vacanamabravi  
  
      Mā tvaṃ bhāyi mahārāja mā tvaṃ bhāyi rathesabha  
 Ahaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi rāhugahitaṃva   candimaṃ

 Ahaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi rāhugahitaṃva suriyaṃ

 Ahaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi peḷābaddhaṃva pantagaṃ

 Ahaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi pakkhiṃ baddhaṃva pañajare

 Ahaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi macche jālagateriva

 Ahaṃ taṃ mocayissāmi sayoggabalavāhanaṃ

 Pañcālaṃ vāhayissāmi kākasenaṃva leḍḍunā  
  
      Dādu paññā kimatthiyā amacco vāpi tādiso  
 Yo taṃ sambādhapakkhannaṃ dukkhā na parimocaye  
  
   Vuṭṭhaṃ   machasaṃ   Ubbedhati   machasaṃ vi   Rāhuggataṃva   machasaṃ 
 Rāhuggahitaṃva   syā  
  
                    
                    
      Etha māṇavā uṭṭhetha mukha ṃsodhatha sandhino vedeho sahamaccehi 
 ummaggena   gamissati  
  
      Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā paṇḍitassānusārino  
 Ummaggadvāraṃ vivariṃsu yantayutte ca aggaḷe  
  
                    
      Purato senako yāti pacchato ca mahosadho  
 Majjhe ca rājā vedeho amaccaparivārito  
  
      Ummaggā   nikkhamitvāna vedeho nāvamāruhi  
 Abhirūḷhañca taṃ ñatvā anusāsi mahosadho  
  
      Ahaṃ te sāsuro   deva ayaṃ sassu janādhipa  
 Yathā mātu paṭipatti evaṃ te hotu sassuyā  
  
      Yathāpi niyako bhātā saudariyo ekamātuko  
 Evaṃ pañcālacaṇḍo te dayitabbo rathesabha  
      Ayaṃ pañcālacaṇḍi te rājaputti abhijjhitā  
 Kāmaṃ karohi te tāya bhariyā te rathesabha  
  
                    
      Ārūyha nāvaṃ taramāno kinnu tīrambhi tiṭṭhasi  
 Kicchā muttambha dukkhāto yāmadāni mahosadha  
  
      Nesa dhammo mahārāja yohaṃ senāya nāyako  
 Senaṅgaṃ parihāpetvā attānaṃ parimocaye  
  
      Nivesanambhi te deva senaṅgaṃ parihāpitaṃ  
 Taṃ dinnaṃ brahmadattena anāyissaṃ rathesabha  
  
      Appaseno mahāsenaṃ kathaṃ viggayha ṭhassasi  
 Dubbalo balavantena vihaññissasi paṇḍita  
  
                    
      Appasenopi ce manti mahāsenaṃ amantinaṃ  
 Jināti   rājā rājāno ādiccovudayaṃ tamaṃ  
  
      Susukhaṃ vata saṃvāso paṇḍitehiti senaka pakkhiva pañajare baddhe   macche 
 jālagateriva 
 Amittahatthatthagate mocayī no mahosadho  
  
   Umaṅgena   machasaṃ ummaṅgena   syā   Umaṅgā   machasaṃ 
   Sayusuro   sīmu machasaṃ syā   Jānātha   machasaṃ 
   Bandhe   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Evametaṃ mahārāja paṇḍitā hi sukhāvahā  
 Pakkhiva pañajare baddhe macche jālagateriva  
 Amittahatthagate mocayī no mahosadho  
                    
      Rakkhitvā kasiṇaṃ rattiṃ cuḷaniyo mahabbalo  
 Udentaṃ aruṇuggamahi upakāriṃ upāgami  
  
      Ārūyha pavaraṃ nāgaṃ balavantaṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ  
 Rājā avoca pañcālo cuḷaniyo mahabbalo  
  
      Sannaddho maṇivammena saramādāya pāṇinā  
 Pessiye ajjhābhāsittha puthugumbe samāgate  
  
      Hatthārūhe anikaṭṭhe rathike pattika rake  
 Upāsanamhi katahatthe vāḷavedhe samāgate  
  
      Pesetha kuñajare danti balavante saṭṭhihāyane  
 Maddantu kuñajarā nagaraṃ   vedehena sumāpitaṃ  
  
      Vacchadantamukhā setā tikhiṇaggā   aṭṭhīvedhino  
 Panunnā dhanuvegena sampatantu tirītaraṃ 
  
      Māṇavā vammino surā citradaṇḍayutāvudhā  
 Pakkhandino mahānāgā hatthinaṃ hontu sammukhā  
  
      Sattiyo teladhotāyo accimantī   pabhassarā  
 Vijjotamānā tiṭṭhantu sataraṃsā viya tārakā  
  
                    
      Āvudhabalavantānaṃ guṇikāyuradhārinaṃ  
 Etādisānaṃ yodhānaṃ saṅgāme apalāyinaṃ  
 Vedeho kuto muccissati sace pakkhiva kāhati   
  
      Tiṃsa me purisanāvutyo sabbe vekekanicchitā    
 Yesaṃ samaṃ na passāmi kevalaṃ mahimaṃ caraṃ  
  
      Nāgā ca kappitā   danti balavanto saṭṭhibhāyanā  
 Yesaṃ khandhesu sobhanti kumārā cārudassanā  
  
      Pītālaṅkārā pitavasanā pituttaranivāsanā  
 Nāgakkhandhesu sobhanti devaputtāva nandane  
  
   Maddantu kuñajaraṃ nāgaṃ   machasaṃ   Kāhiti   machasaṃ vi  
   Tiṇugga   machasaṃ   Naccitā   machasaṃ 
   Taritarā   machasaṃ   Kappakā   machasaṃ 
   Accimantā   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Pāṭhinavaṇṇā   nettiṃsā teladhotā pabhassarā  
 Niṭṭhitā naravirehi   samadhārā sunissitā   
  
      Vellālino vitamalā sikkāyasmayā daḷhā  
 Gahitā balavantehi suppahārapapahārinā  
  
      Suvaṇṇatharusampannā lohitakacchupadhāritā  
 Vivattamātā sobanti vijjuvabbhaghanantare  
  
      Patākā   vammino surā asicammassa kovidā  
 Tharūggahā   sikkhitāro nāgakkhandhātipātino   
  
      Edisehi   parikkhitto natthi mokkho ito tava  
 Pabhāvaṃ te na passāmi yena tvaṃ mithilaṃ vaje  
  
                    
      Kinnu santaramānova nāgaṃ pesesi kuñajaraṃ  
 Pahaṭṭharūpo āpatasi   laddhatthosmīti   maññasi  
  
      Oharetaṃ    dhanu cāpaṃ khurappaṃ paṭisaṃhara  
 Ośaretaṃ subhaṃ cammaṃ veḷuriyamaṇiyanthataṃ    
  
      Pasannamukhavaṇṇosi mihitapubbañca bhāsasi  
 Hoti kho maraṇakāle tādisi    vaṇṇasampadā

 Duggaṇho hi tayā rājā khaḷuṅkeneva    sindhavo  
  
      Tiṇṇe hiyyo rājā gaṅgaṃ sāmacco saparijjano  
 Haṃsarājaṃ yathā dhaṅko anujjavaṃ papatissasi

 Maṃsapesīti maññantā pirabbuḷhā migādhamā

 Yo me amittaṃ hatthagataṃ vedehaṃ parimocayi

 Yo me amittaṃ hatthagataṃ vedehaṃ parimocayi
